 unka janm 22 janvari ko 1908 main hua tha

 aaj kii janareshan bhale hi unhen na jaanati ho lekin vah aise shaks the jinhone physics ke kshetra main kaaphi avishkaar or yogadan diya tha
 In the year 1962, he was awarded the Nobel Prize in Physics
 bataa den, unhen ye puraskaar behad kam taapmaana par liquid (taral) helium ke vyavhaar par shodh karne par diya gaya tha
 Lev Landau had an interest in mathematics and science since childhood

 jahaan unhone rockfilor scolership hasil kii or bataur vaigyanik apane kariyar kii shuruyaat kii
